"arm and elbow, external approach. this class includes one or more of 16 standard surgical interventions or procedures on component parts of the arm and elbow, via external approach.  these surgical interventions or procedures are listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 pcs under code 0x.. .
